The application will automatically graph the load versus equivalent core diameter and automatically calculate the unconfined compressive strength for the rock specimen.\r\n\r\nNew specimen dimensions are automatically measured and recorded as well as starting a new test using a load value threshold. After performing a test, the application will automatically record the data and begin a new test. This allows many tests to be completed in the same time it would normally take for one test to be performed on a standard device, as all data recording is performed by the application.
